20107 = {
	name="Hodor"	# The Red Kraken.
	dynasty=107
	
	dna = wkyjyadlsrn
	properties = difb0k0b0000
	
	martial = 9
	diplomacy=7
	intrigue=9
	stewardship=4
	learning=3

	religion="drowned_god"
	culture="ironborn"
	
	father=21107 # Vickon Greyjoy
	mother=41107
	
	#add_trait=proud
	add_trait=wroth
	add_trait=ruthless
	add_trait=ambitious
	add_trait=brave
	add_trait=lustful
	add_trait=stubborn
	add_trait=tough_soldier
	
	add_trait=inspiring_leader
	
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	
	8113.1.1 = {birth="8113.1.1"  }
	8123.1.1 = { #already reaving
		add_trait=trained_warrior  
		effect = {
			add_friend=195107 #his uncle
		}
	}
	8127.1.1 = { #stole sword from a corsair and took many salt wives
		add_trait=nightfall
		remove_trait=trained_warrior  
		add_trait=skilled_warrior
		add_trait=viking
		effect = { 
			prestige = 150 
			piety = 75
			wealth = 100
		}
	}
	8128.3.2 = { #avenged uncle's death
		add_trait=scarred
		give_nickname = nick_the_red_kraken
		effect = { 
			prestige = 300
			piety = 150
			wealth = 100
		}
	}
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			character_event = { id = dance_of_dragons.17 }
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {
		death={
			death_reason=death_murder
			killer=395194
		}
	}
}
#Salt wives
490107 = {
	name="Hodor"
	female=yes

	religion="corsair"
	culture = summer_islander
	
	add_trait=fair
	add_trait=amateurish_plotter

	8113.1.1 = {
		birth="8113.1.1"
		effect = {
			dynasty = none
		}
	}
	8127.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			add_trait = salt_wife
			c_pyke = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { move_character = PREV }
				}
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { character = 20107 }
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "The Old Gods" } }#Uses new DLC system instead if owned
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_salt_wife
							who = PREV
							years = 100
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_dlc = "The Old Gods" } #Uses new DLC system instead if owned
						add_consort = PREV
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_forced_consort
							who = PREV
						}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	8150.1.1 = {death="8150.1.1"}
}
